				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Johannespassion, BWV 245 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts, 40 (NBA) or 68 (BWV) numbers
<ul><li><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/St_John_Passion_structure" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:St John Passion structure"><i>Detailed listing</i></a>
</li></ul>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1724, rev.1725, 1728-32, 1749, 1739-49 (final form, never performed during Bach's lifetime)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<tr>
<th>Editor
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Mendel,_Arthur" title="Category:Mendel, Arthur">Arthur Mendel</a>&#160;(1905-1979)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Pub<span class="mh555">lisher</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Info.
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Neue_Bach-Ausgabe_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Neue Bach-Ausgabe (Bach, Johann Sebastian)"><i>Neue Bach-Ausgabe</i></a>, <i>Serie II. <th>Name Translations
